$egesli:c/aj_EI[SE]+LICHE $-ly/xs-aj_+LICHE
{=SE have been erased, whether by Scribe A himself or some other is not}
{certain. The letters are still partially visible. Given Scribe B´s}
{spelling, also EISELICHE, I have chosen to regard the correction as not}
{by Scribe A, who is in any case a literatim copyist by habit. The}
{spelling EISELICHE would seem therefore to represent the spelling of the}
{exemplar which is what, for the most part, is represented by Scribe A´s work}
{as a whole. I therefore keep Scribe A´s original spelling here. Note}
{that Morris (1873) reads EI[S]LICHE but the remains of both S and E are clear=}
{.}
